This set of rules makes it\n    23→// possible to control which modifications a filter may make.\n    24→//\n    25→// By default, an external processing server may add, modify, or remove\n    26→// any header except for an \"Envoy internal\" header (which is typically\n    27→// denoted by an x-envoy prefix) or specific headers that may affect\n    28→// further filter processing:\n    29→//\n    30→// * ``host``\n    31→// * ``:authority``\n    32→// * ``:scheme``\n    33→// * ``:method``\n    34→//\n    35→// Every attempt to add, change, append, or remove a header will be\n    36→// tested against the rules here.
